                    iframe.style.height = &#39;100%&#39;;

                    iframe.src = url;
                    win.document.body.appendChild(iframe);
                    

                    var interval = setInterval(function() {
                        if (win.closed) {
                            clearInterval(interval);
                            win = undefined;

                        }
                    }, 500);


                }
            };
        }
